2026-06-26 13:59:11,118 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 13:59:11,198 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine [cached since 0.1277s ago] ('a1111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111',)
2026-06-26 13:59:11,198 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 13:59:11,198 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 13:59:11,308 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

        SELECT tp.id AS plan_id, tp.patient_id, p.name AS patient_name, p.phone,
               tp.followup_date,
               (CAST($1 AS date) - tp.followup_date) AS days_overdue,
               tp.followup_notes,
               COALESCE(tp.plan_name, tp.name) AS plan_name
        FROM treatment_plans tp
        JOIN patients p ON p.id = tp.patient_id
        WHERE tp.clinic_id = $2
          AND tp.followup_date IS NOT NULL
          AND tp.followup_date <= $1
          AND COALESCE(tp.status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ORDER BY tp.followup_date ASC
        LIMIT $3

        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 13:59:42,215 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine [cached since 31.13s ago] ('pending', UUID('a1111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111'))
2026-06-26 13:59:42,215 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 13:59:42,215 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:00:12,140 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 14:00:12,140 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:00:42,156 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:01:12,158 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:01:42,145 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:02:12,146 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 14:02:12,146 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:03:18,182 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:03:37,789 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:03:42,644 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 14:03:42,644 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:03:42,916 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 14:03:42,916 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:03:50,437 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count

2026-06-26 14:04:20,433 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine BEGIN (implicit)
2026-06-26 14:04:20,433 INFO sqlalchemy.engine.Engine 
        WITH apt_today AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $2
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        apt_tom AS (
          SELECT bucket, COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND effective_date = $3
          GROUP BY bucket
        ),
        rev AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(amount),0) AS revenue_today
          FROM payment_transactions
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND date = $2
        ),
        out_total AS (
          SELECT COALESCE(SUM(balance),0) AS outstanding_total
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND balance > 0
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        ),
        lab_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status IN ('pending','sent','received')
        ),
        lab_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM lab_orders
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND status IN ('pending','sent')
            AND expected_date IS NOT NULL
            AND expected_date < $2
        ),
        unscheduled AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM v_appointments_bucketed
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND bucket = 'unscheduled'
            AND effective_date >= $2 - INTERVAL '7 days'
        ),
        reschedule_pending AS (
          SELECT COUNT(*) AS n
          FROM reschedule_requests
          WHERE clinic_id = $1 AND status = 'pending'
        ),
        followups_overdue AS (
          SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT patient_id) AS n
          FROM treatment_plans
          WHERE clinic_id = $1
            AND followup_date IS NOT NULL
            AND followup_date < $2
            AND COALESCE(status,'') NOT IN ('cancelled','closed')
        )
        SELECT
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today) AS appts_today_total,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='in_clinic') AS appts_today_in_clinic,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='completed') AS appts_today_completed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='confirmed') AS appts_today_confirmed,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_today WHERE bucket='unscheduled') AS appts_today_unscheduled,
          (SELECT COALESCE(SUM(n),0) FROM apt_tom)   AS appts_tomorrow_total,
          (SELECT revenue_today FROM rev),
          (SELECT outstanding_total FROM out_total),
          (SELECT n FROM lab_pending) AS lab_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM lab_overdue) AS lab_overdue_count,
          (SELECT n FROM unscheduled) AS unscheduled_recent_count,
          (SELECT n FROM reschedule_pending) AS reschedule_pending_count,
          (SELECT n FROM followups_overdue) AS followups_overdue_count
